## Description

Product information

## BaerCoil Spark Plug Thread Repair Kit M 10 x 1.0

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair spark plug threads or glow plug threads in MF 10 x 1.0.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the combination tap with guide thread, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. For spark plug threads, no reaming is necessary because the combined drilling and cutting tool is used here. The hole is widened by the guide thread and then the thread is cut with oversize. For spark plug threads, the tang must be removed with needle-nose pliers.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened if necessary, according to the required length, with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 10 |
| Pitch | 1,0 |
| Dimension | MF 10 x 1,0 |
| Length | 1,0 D \| 1,5 D \| 2,0 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 1,0 D: 10 mm \| 1,5 D: 15 mm \| 2,0 D: 20 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 10 mm=15 mm<br>The nominal diameter for MF 10 is 10 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | MF: Metric ISO fine thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

Thread repair and thread reinforcement of spark plug threads.

### Technical drawing

![](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 10 |
| Length | 1,0 D \| 1,5 D \| 2,0 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 1,0 D: 10 mm \| 1,5 D: 15 mm \| 2,0 D: 20 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 11,17 mm - 12,50 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |

### Content

- 1 x B3632: BaerCoil HSSG combination tap for spark plugs M 10 x 1.0 EG
- 1 x EBW10: BaerCoil Installation tool M 10 x 1.0
- 5 x B7217-1: BaerCoil thread inserts M 10 x 1,0 - length: 1,0 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)
- 5 x B7217-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 10 x 1.0 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free flowing" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)
- 5 x B7217-2: BaerCoil thread inserts M 10 x 1.0 - length: 2.0 D - type: "free flowing" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

BAERCOIL


## M 10 x 1.0 Spark Plug BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit for (Helicoil Type)

**$89.00** ~~~~

Product information

## BaerCoil Spark Plug Thread Repair Kit M 10 x 1.0

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair spark plug threads or glow plug threads in MF 10 x 1.0.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the combination tap with guide thread, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. For spark plug threads, no reaming is necessary because the combined drilling and cutting tool is used here. The hole is widened by the guide thread and then the thread is cut with oversize. For spark plug threads, the tang must be removed with needle-nose pliers.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened if necessary, according to the required length, with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 10 |
| Pitch | 1,0 |
| Dimension | MF 10 x 1,0 |
| Length | 1,0 D \| 1,5 D \| 2,0 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 1,0 D: 10 mm \| 1,5 D: 15 mm \| 2,0 D: 20 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 10 mm=15 mm<br>The nominal diameter for MF 10 is 10 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | MF: Metric ISO fine thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

Thread repair and thread reinforcement of spark plug threads.

### Technical drawing

![](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 10 |
| Length | 1,0 D \| 1,5 D \| 2,0 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 1,0 D: 10 mm \| 1,5 D: 15 mm \| 2,0 D: 20 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 11,17 mm - 12,50 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |

### Content

- 1 x B3632: BaerCoil HSSG combination tap for spark plugs M 10 x 1.0 EG
- 1 x EBW10: BaerCoil Installation tool M 10 x 1.0
- 5 x B7217-1: BaerCoil thread inserts M 10 x 1,0 - length: 1,0 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)
- 5 x B7217-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 10 x 1.0 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free flowing" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)
- 5 x B7217-2: BaerCoil thread inserts M 10 x 1.0 - length: 2.0 D - type: "free flowing" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

## Description

Complete BaerCoil Thread-Repair-Kit Contents: 1 x  HSSG BaerCoil Spark Plug Tap with Pilot Nose (no pre-drilling necessary) 1 x  Inserting Tool + 5 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304) length: 12 mm + 5 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304) length: 18 mm + 5 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304) length: 24 mm

No Tang break tool - for Spark Plug use a longe nose pliers to remove the tang.

[BaerCoil instruction for use](http://www.baercoil.com/en/instructions_baercoil_spark_plug.html) [Technical data - metric BaerCoil wire thread inserts DIN 8140](http://www.baercoil.com/en/dimensions_metric.html) [Drill Sizes](http://www.baercoil.com/en/drill_sizes.html) [Technical Information](http://www.baercoil.com/en/baercoil_technical_info.html)

BaerCoil: - Thread Repair of damaged or worn-out threads - Recovery of rejected items - Thread Armour Plating. For material with low shear strenght eg. aluminium alloys and magnesium alloys.

Due to narrow and exact tolerances the new thread normally is stronger than the original one. Use in machine-building, electrical, automotive, medical and aerospace industries.

## Description

Product information

## BaerCoil Spark Plug Thread Repair Kit M 14 x 1.25

* * *

With this BaerCoil® thread repair-set it is possible to repair spark plug threads or glow plug threads in MF 14 x 1,25.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the combination tap with guide thread, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. For spark plug threads, no reaming is necessary because the combined drilling and cutting tool is used here. The hole is widened by the guide thread and then the thread is cut with oversize. For spark plug threads, the tang must be removed with needle-nose pliers.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened if necessary, according to the required length, with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 14 |
| Pitch | 1,25 |
| Dimension | MF 14 x 1,25 |
| Length | 8,4 mm \| 12,4 mm \| 16,4 mm |
| T (Length when installed) | 8,4 mm \| 12,4 mm \| 16,4 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 14 mm=21 mm<br>The nominal diameter for MF 14 is 14 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | MF: Metric ISO fine thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

Thread repair and thread reinforcement of spark plug threads.

### Technical drawing

![Technical drawing BaerCoil thread insert](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 14 |
| Length | 8,4 mm \| 12,4 mm \| 16,4 mm |
| T (Length when installed) | 8,4 mm \| 12,4 mm \| 16,4 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 15,47 mm - 17,03 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |

## Description

Complete BaerCoil Thread-Repair-Kit Contents: 1 x  HSSG BaerCoil Spark Plug Tap with Pilot Nose (no pre-drilling necessary) 1 x  Inserting Tool + 5 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304) length: 12.7 mm + 5 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304) length: 15.9 mm + 5 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304) length: 16.7 mm

No Tang break tool - for Spark Plug use a longe nose pliers to remove the tang.

[BaerCoil instruction for use](http://www.baercoil.com/en/instructions_baercoil_spark_plug.html) [Technical data - metric BaerCoil wire thread inserts DIN 8140](http://www.baercoil.com/en/dimensions_metric.html) [Drill Sizes](http://www.baercoil.com/en/drill_sizes.html) [Technical Information](http://www.baercoil.com/en/baercoil_technical_info.html)

BaerCoil: - Thread Repair of damaged or worn-out threads - Recovery of rejected items - Thread Armour Plating. For material with low shear strenght eg. aluminium alloys and magnesium alloys.

Due to narrow and exact tolerances the new thread normally is stronger than the original one. Use in machine-building, electrical, automotive, medical and aerospace industries.

## M 18 x 1.5 Spark Plug BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit for (Helicoil Type)

**$131.00** ~~~~

Complete BaerCoil Thread-Repair-Kit Contents: 1 x  HSSG BaerCoil Spark Plug Tap with Pilot Nose (no pre-drilling necessary) 1 x  Inserting Tool + 5 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304) length: 12.7 mm + 5 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304) length: 15.9 mm + 5 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304) length: 16.7 mm

No Tang break tool - for Spark Plug use a longe nose pliers to remove the tang.

[BaerCoil instruction for use](http://www.baercoil.com/en/instructions_baercoil_spark_plug.html) [Technical data - metric BaerCoil wire thread inserts DIN 8140](http://www.baercoil.com/en/dimensions_metric.html) [Drill Sizes](http://www.baercoil.com/en/drill_sizes.html) [Technical Information](http://www.baercoil.com/en/baercoil_technical_info.html)

BaerCoil: - Thread Repair of damaged or worn-out threads - Recovery of rejected items - Thread Armour Plating. For material with low shear strenght eg. aluminium alloys and magnesium alloys.

Due to narrow and exact tolerances the new thread normally is stronger than the original one. Use in machine-building, electrical, automotive, medical and aerospace industries.

## Description

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 10 x 1.0

With this BaerCoil® thread repair-set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in MF 10 x 1.0.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair kit contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool, tang breaker and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, according to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 10 |
| Pitch | 1,0 |
| Dimension | MF 10 x 1,0 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 15 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 10 mm=15 mm<br>The nominal diameter for MF 10 is 10 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | MF: Metric ISO fine thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 10 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 15 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 11,17 mm - 12,50 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 18,50 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 19,50 mm |

### Content

- 1 x 161103: BaerCoil HSS twist drill bit 10.30 mm
- 1 x B3017-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 10 x 1.0 EG
- 1 x EBW10: BaerCoil Installation tool M 10 x 1.0
- 1 x BZ010: BaerCoil Tang breaker M 10 x 1.0
- 15 x B7217-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 10 x 1.0 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

## Description

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 10 x 1.25

With this BaerCoil® thread repair-set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in MF 10 x 1,25.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair kit contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool, tang breaker and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, according to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 10 |
| Pitch | 1,25 |
| Dimension | MF 10 x 1,25 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 15 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 10 mm=15 mm<br>The nominal diameter for MF 10 is 10 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | MF: Metric ISO fine thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 10 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 15 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 11,45 mm - 12,65 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 19,38 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 20,63 mm |

### Content

- 1 x 161103: BaerCoil HSS twist drill bit 10.30 mm
- 1 x B3016-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 10 x 1.25 EG
- 1 x EBW10: BaerCoil Installation tool M 10 x 1.25
- 1 x BZ010: BaerCoil Tang breaker M 10 x 1,25
- 15 x B7216-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 10 x 1.25 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

BAERCOIL


## M10 X 1.5 BaerCoil Kit (Helicoil Type)

**$69.00** ~~~~

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 10 x 1.5

With this BaerCoil® thread repair-set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in M 10 x 1.5.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair kit contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool, tang breaker and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, according to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 10 |
| Pitch | 1,5 |
| Dimension | M 10 x 1,5 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 15 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 10 mm=15 mm<br>The nominal diameter for M 10 is 10 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | M: Metric ISO standard thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 10 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 15 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 11,74 mm - 12,50 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 20,25 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 21,75 mm |

### Content

- 1 x 161104: BaerCoil HSS twist drill bit 10.40 mm
- 1 x B3015-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 10 x 1.5 EG
- 1 x EBW10: BaerCoil Installation tool M 10 x 1.5
- 1 x BZ010: BaerCoil Tang breaker M 10 x 1,5
- 15 x B7215-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 10 x 1.5 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

- TRS M10 X 1.5 KIT

## Description

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 11 x 1.25

* * *

With this BaerCoil® thread repair-set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in MF 11 x 1.25.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair kit contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool, tang breaker and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, according to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 11 |
| Pitch | 1,25 |
| Dimension | MF 11 x 1,25 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 16,5 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 11 mm=16.5 mm<br>The nominal diameter for MF 11 is 11 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | MF: Metric ISO fine thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![Technical drawing BaerCoil thread insert](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 11 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 16,5 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 12,47 mm - 13,76 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 20,87 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 22,12 mm |

### Content

- 1 x 161113: BaerCoil HSS twist drill bit 11.30 mm
- 1 x B3075-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 11 x 1.25 EG
- 1 x EBW10: BaerCoil installation tool M 11 x 1.25
- 1 x BZ010: BaerCoil Tang breaker M 11 x 1,25
- 5 x BE1125-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 11 x 1.25 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

## M11 X 1.5 BaerCoil Kit (Helicoil Type)

**$79.00** ~~~~

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 11 x 1.5

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind-hole threads in M 11 x 1.5.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair kit contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool, tang breaker and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, according to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 11 |
| Pitch | 1,5 |
| Dimension | M 11 x 1,5 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 16,5 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 11 mm=16.5 mm<br>The nominal diameter for M 11 is 11 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | M: Metric ISO standard thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 11 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 16,5 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 12,74 mm - 13,59 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 21,75 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 23,25 mm |

### Content

- 1 x 161113: BaerCoil HSS twist drill bit 11.30 mm
- 1 x B3018-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 11 x 1.5 EG
- 1 x EBW10: BaerCoil installation tool M 11 x 1.5
- 1 x BZ010: BaerCoil Tang breaker M 11 x 1.5
- 10 x B7219-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 11 x 1.5 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

BAERCOIL


## M12 X 1.25 BaerCoil Kit (Helicoil Type)

**$81.00** ~~~~

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 12 x 1.25

With this BaerCoil® thread repair-set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in MF 12 x 1.25.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair kit contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool, tang breaker and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, according to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 12 |
| Pitch | 1,25 |
| Dimension | MF 12 x 1,25 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 18 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 12 mm=18 mm<br>The nominal diameter for MF 12 is 12 mm |

### Characteristics

| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

## Description

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 12 x 1.75

With this BaerCoil® thread repair-set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in M 12 x 1.75.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair kit contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool, tang breaker and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, according to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 12 |
| Pitch | 1,75 |
| Dimension | M 12 x 1,75 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 18 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 12 mm=18 mm<br>The nominal diameter for M 12 is 12 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | M: Metric ISO standard thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 12 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 18 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 14,03 mm - 15,00 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 24,13 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 25,88 mm |

### Content

- 1 x 161124: BaerCoil HSS twist drill bit 12.40 mm
- 1 x B3020-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 12 x 1.75 EG
- 1 x EBW12: BaerCoil Installation tool M 12 x 1.75
- 1 x BZ012: BaerCoil Tang breaker M 12 x 1,75
- 10 x B7221-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 12 x 1.75 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 13 x 1.25

With this BaerCoil® thread repair-set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in MF 13 x 1.25.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

No tang breaker is included in this set. The tang can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull back the installation tool after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tang. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

BAERCOIL


## M13 X 1.25 BaerCoil Kit (Helicoil Type)

**$244.00** ~~~~

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 13 x 1.25

With this BaerCoil® thread repair-set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in MF 13 x 1.25.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

No tang breaker is included in this set. The tang can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull back the installation tool after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tang. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 13 |
| Pitch | 1,25 |
| Dimension | MF 13 x 1,25 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 19,5 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 13 mm=19.5 mm<br>The nominal diameter for MF 13 is 13 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | MF: Metric ISO fine thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

## Description

Complete BaerCoil Thread-Repair-Kit

Content:

1 x M14.4 BaerCoil Drill Bit

1 x HSSG BaerCoil Tap > ISO1-4H

1 x BaerCoil Inserting Tool

\+ 10 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304), lenght: 1,5 x D

BaerCoil:

\- Thread Repair of damaged or worn-out threads

\- Recovery of rejected items

\- Thread Armour Plating. For material with low shear

strenght eg. aluminium alloys and magnesium alloys.

Due to narrow and exact tolerances the new thread

normally is stronger than the original one.

Use in machine-building, electrical, automotive,

medical and aerospace industries.

## Description

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 14 x 1.25

With this BaerCoil® thread repair-set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in MF 14 x 1.25.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

No tang breaker is included in this set. The tang can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull back the installation tool after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tang. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 14 |
| Pitch | 1,25 |
| Dimension | MF 14 x 1,25 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 21 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 14 mm=21 mm<br>The nominal diameter for MF 14 is 14 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | MF: Metric ISO fine thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 14 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 21 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 15,47 mm - 17,03 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 25,37 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 26,62 mm |

### Content

- 1 x 111144: BaerCoil HSS twist drill bit with countersunk shank 14.40 mm
- 1 x B3029-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 14 x 1.25 EG
- 1 x EBW14: BaerCoil installation tool M 14 x 1,25
- 10 x B7227-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 14 x 1.25 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

BAERCOIL


## M14 X 1.25 BaerCoil Kit (Helicoil Type)

**$91.00** ~~~~

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 14 x 1.25

With this BaerCoil® thread repair-set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in MF 14 x 1.25.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

No tang breaker is included in this set. The tang can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull back the installation tool after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tang. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 14 |
| Pitch | 1,25 |
| Dimension | MF 14 x 1,25 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 21 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 14 mm=21 mm<br>The nominal diameter for MF 14 is 14 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | MF: Metric ISO fine thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 14 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 21 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 15,47 mm - 17,03 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 25,37 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 26,62 mm |

### Content

- 1 x 111144: BaerCoil HSS twist drill bit with countersunk shank 14.40 mm
- 1 x B3029-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 14 x 1.25 EG
- 1 x EBW14: BaerCoil installation tool M 14 x 1,25
- 10 x B7227-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 14 x 1.25 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

Style

- BAERCOIL M14 X 1.25 KIT

## Description

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 14 x 2.0

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind-hole threads in M 14 x 2.0.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

No tang breaker is included in this set. The tang can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull back the installation tool after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tang. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 14 |
| Pitch | 2,0 |
| Dimension | M 14 x 2,0 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 21 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 14 mm=21 mm<br>The nominal diameter for M 14 is 14 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | M: Metric ISO standard thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 14 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 21 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 16,31 mm - 17,35 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 28,00 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 30,00 mm |

### Content

- 1 x 111144: BaerCoil HSS twist drill bit with countersunk shank 14.40 mm
- 1 x B3027-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 14 x 2.0 EG
- 1 x EBW14: BaerCoil installation tool M 14 x 2.0
- 10 x B7225-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 14 x 2.0 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 15 x 1.5

* * *

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in MF 15 x 1.5.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the hand tap with oversize for insert threads, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. To drill the core hole, a 15.5 mm twist drill bit is still needed here. The tenon can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull the installation tool back after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tenon. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

BAERCOIL


## M15 X 1.5 BaerCoil Kit (Helicoil Type)

**$233.00** ~~~~

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 15 x 1.5

* * *

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in MF 15 x 1.5.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the hand tap with oversize for insert threads, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. To drill the core hole, a 15.5 mm twist drill bit is still needed here. The tenon can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull the installation tool back after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tenon. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 15 |
| Pitch | 1,5 |
| Dimension | MF 15 x 1,5 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 22,5 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 15 mm=22.5 mm<br>The nominal diameter for MF 15 is 15 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | MF: Metric ISO fine thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![Technical drawing BaerCoil thread insert](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 15 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 22,5 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |

### Content

- 1 x B3079-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 15 x 1.5 EG
- 1 x EBW14: BaerCoil Installation tool M 15 x 1.5
- 5 x BE1515-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 15 x 1.5 - length: 1.5 D - type: free-running - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

## Description

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 16 x 2.0

* * *

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind-hole threads in M 16 x 2.0.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the hand tap with oversize for insert threads, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. To drill the core hole, a 16.5 mm twist drill bit is still needed here. The tenon can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull the installation tool back after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tenon. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 16 |
| Pitch | 2,0 |
| Dimension | M 16 x 2,0 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 24 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 16 mm=24 mm<br>The nominal diameter for M 16 is 16 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | M: Metric ISO standard thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

## M16 X 2.0 BaerCoil Kit (Helicoil Type)

**$103.00** ~~~~

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 16 x 2.0

* * *

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind-hole threads in M 16 x 2.0.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the hand tap with oversize for insert threads, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. To drill the core hole, a 16.5 mm twist drill bit is still needed here. The tenon can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull the installation tool back after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tenon. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 16 |
| Pitch | 2,0 |
| Dimension | M 16 x 2,0 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 24 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 16 mm=24 mm<br>The nominal diameter for M 16 is 16 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | M: Metric ISO standard thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

| Diameter | 16 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 24 mm |

| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 33,00 mm |

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the hand tap with oversize for insert threads, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. To drill the core hole, an 18.5 mm twist drill bit is still needed here. The tenon can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull the installation tool back after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tenon. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 18 x 2.5

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind-hole threads in M 18 x 2.5.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the hand tap with oversize for insert threads, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. To drill the core hole, an 18.5 mm twist drill bit is still needed here. The tenon can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull the installation tool back after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tenon. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

BAERCOIL


## M18 X 2.5 BaerCoil Kit (Helicoil Type)

**$141.00** ~~~~

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 18 x 2.5

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind-hole threads in M 18 x 2.5.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the hand tap with oversize for insert threads, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. To drill the core hole, an 18.5 mm twist drill bit is still needed here. The tenon can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull the installation tool back after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tenon. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 18 |
| Pitch | 2,5 |
| Dimension | M 18 x 2,5 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 27 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 18 mm=27 mm<br>The nominal diameter for M 18 is 18 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | M: Metric ISO standard thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 18 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 27 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 20,86 mm - 22,00 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 35,75 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 38,25 mm |

### Content

- 1 x B3035-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 18 x 2.5 EG
- 1 x EBW18: BaerCoil Installation tool M 18 x 2.5
- 5 x B7236-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 18 x 2.5 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

- TRS M18 X 2.5 KIT
- BAERCOIL M18 X 2.5 KIT

BaerCoil:

\- Recovery of rejected items

\- Thread Armour Plating. For material with low shear

strenght eg. aluminium alloys and magnesium alloys.

normally is stronger than the original one.

Use in machine-building, electrical, automotive,

medical and aerospace industries.
