## Description

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 2.5 x 0.45

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole and blind-hole threads in M 2.5 x 0.45.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair kit contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool, tang breaker and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, according to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 2,5 |
| Pitch | 0,45 |
| Dimension | M 2,5 x 0,45 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 3,75 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 2.5 mm=3.75 mm<br>The nominal diameter for M 2.5 is 2.5 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | M: Metric ISO standard thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 2,5 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 3,75 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 3,04 mm - 3,70 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 5,33 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 5,78 mm |

### Content

- 1 x 16126: BaerCoil HSS twist drill bit 2.60 mm
- 1 x B3003-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 2.5 x 0.45 EG
- 1 x EBW02: BaerCoil Installation tool M 2.5 x 0.45
- 1 x BZ002: BaerCoil Tang breaker M 2,5 x 0,45
- 20 x B7204-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 2,5 x 0,45 - length: 1,5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

## Description

Complete BaerCoil Thread-Repair-Kit

Content:

1 x M2.1 BaerCoil Drill Bit

1 x HSSG BaerCoil Tap > ISO1-4H

1 x BaerCoil Inserting Tool

1 x BaerCoil Tang Break Tool

\+ 20 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304), lenght: 1,5 x D

BaerCoil:

\- Thread Repair of damaged or worn-out threads

\- Recovery of rejected items

\- Thread Armour Plating. For material with low shear

strenght eg. aluminium alloys and magnesium alloys.

Due to narrow and exact tolerances the new thread

normally is stronger than the original one.

Use in machine-building, electrical, automotive,

medical and aerospace industries.

## Description

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 20 x 1.5

* * *

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in MF 20 x 1.5.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the hand tap with oversize for insert threads, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. To drill the core hole, a 20.5 mm twist drill bit is still needed here. The tenon can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull the installation tool back after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tenon. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 20 |
| Pitch | 1,5 |
| Dimension | MF 20 x 1,5 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 30 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 20 mm=30 mm<br>The nominal diameter for MF 20 is 20 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | MF: Metric ISO fine thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![Technical drawing BaerCoil thread insert](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 20 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 30 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 21,75 mm - 24,00 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 35,25 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 36,75 mm |

### Content

- 1 x B3040-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 20 x 1.5 EG
- 1 x EBW20: BaerCoil Installation tool M 20 x 1.5
- 5 x B7241-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 20 x 1.5 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

## M20 X 2.0 BaerCoil Kit (Helicoil Type)

Complete BaerCoil Thread-Repair-Kit

Content:

1 x HSSG BaerCoil Tap > ISO1-4H

1 x BaerCoil Inserting Tool

\+ 5 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304), lenght: 1,5 x D

BaerCoil:

\- Recovery of rejected items

\- Thread Armour Plating. For material with low shear

## Description

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 22 x 1.5

* * *

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in MF 22 x 1.5.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the hand tap with oversize for insert threads, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. To drill the core hole, a 22.5 mm twist drill bit is still needed here. The tenon can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull the installation tool back after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tenon. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 22 |
| Pitch | 1,5 |
| Dimension | MF 22 x 1,5 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 33 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 22 mm=33 mm<br>The nominal diameter for MF 22 is 22 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | MF: Metric ISO fine thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![Technical drawing BaerCoil thread insert](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 22 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 33 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 23,75 mm - 26,45 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 38,25 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 39,75 mm |

### Content

- 1 x B3043-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 22 x 1.5 EG
- 1 x EBW22: BaerCoil Installation tool M 22 x 1.5
- 5 x B7244-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 22 x 1.5 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

## Description

Complete BaerCoil Thread-Repair-Kit

Content:

1 x HSSG BaerCoil Tap > ISO1-4H

1 x BaerCoil Inserting Tool

\+ 5 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304), lenght: 1,5 x D

BaerCoil:

\- Thread Repair of damaged or worn-out threads

\- Recovery of rejected items

\- Thread Armour Plating. For material with low shear

strenght eg. aluminium alloys and magnesium alloys.

Due to narrow and exact tolerances the new thread

normally is stronger than the original one.

Use in machine-building, electrical, automotive,

medical and aerospace industries.

## Description

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 22 x 2.5

* * *

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind-hole threads in M 22 x 2.5.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the hand tap with oversize for insert threads, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. To drill the core hole, a 22.5 mm twist drill bit is still needed here. The tenon can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull the installation tool back after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tenon. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 22 |
| Pitch | 2,5 |
| Dimension | M 22 x 2,5 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 33 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 22 mm=33 mm<br>The nominal diameter for M 22 is 22 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | M: Metric ISO standard thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![Technical drawing BaerCoil thread insert](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 22 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 33 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 24,86 mm - 26,90 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 41,75 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 44,25 mm |

### Content

- 1 x B3041-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 22 x 2.5 EG
- 1 x EBW22: BaerCoil Installation tool M 22 x 2.5
- 5 x B7242-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 22 x 2.5 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the hand tap with oversize for insert threads, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. To drill the core hole, a 22.5 mm twist drill bit is still needed here. The tenon can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull the installation tool back after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tenon. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 22 |
| Pitch | 2,5 |
| Dimension | M 22 x 2,5 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 33 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 22 mm=33 mm<br>The nominal diameter for M 22 is 22 mm |

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 24 x 1.5

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in MF 24 x 1.5.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the hand tap with oversize for insert threads, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. To drill the core hole, a 24.5 mm twist drill bit is still needed here. The tenon can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull the installation tool back after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tenon. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the hand tap with oversize for insert threads, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. To drill the core hole, a 24.5 mm twist drill bit is still needed here. The tenon can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull the installation tool back after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tenon. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

## M24 X 2.0 BaerCoil Kit (Helicoil Type)

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 24 x 2.0

* * *

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in MF 24 x 2.0.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the hand tap with oversize for insert threads, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. To drill the core hole, a 24.5 mm twist drill bit is still needed here. The tenon can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull the installation tool back after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tenon. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 24 |
| Pitch | 2,0 |
| Dimension | MF 24 x 2,0 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 36 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 24 mm=36 mm<br>The nominal diameter for MF 24 is 24 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |

| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |

| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

BAERCOIL


## M24 X 3.0 BaerCoil Kit (Helicoil Type)

**$214.00** ~~~~

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 24 x 3.0

* * *

With this BaerCoil® thread repair-set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in M 24 x 3.0.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair set contains various auxiliary tools, such as the hand tap with oversize for insert threads, insertion tool and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

This set does not include twist drill bit and tang breaker. To drill the core hole, a 24.5 mm twist drill bit is still needed here. The tenon can be broken with the installation tool. To do this, pull the installation tool back after installation and turn it 90° so that it rests on the tenon. Then strike the tool briefly at the back.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 24 |
| Pitch | 3,0 |
| Dimension | M 24 x 3,0 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 36 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 24 mm=36 mm<br>The nominal diameter for M 24 is 24 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | M: Metric ISO standard thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![Technical drawing of BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 24 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 36 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 27,43 mm - 29,00 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 46,50 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 49,50 mm |

## Description

Complete BaerCoil Thread-Repair-Kit

Content:

1 x M3.7 BaerCoil Drill Bit

1 x HSSG BaerCoil Tap > ISO1-4H

1 x BaerCoil Inserting Tool

1 x BaerCoil Tang Break Tool

\+ 20 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304), lenght: 1,5 x D

BaerCoil:

\- Thread Repair of damaged or worn-out threads

\- Recovery of rejected items

\- Thread Armour Plating. For material with low shear

strenght eg. aluminium alloys and magnesium alloys.

Due to narrow and exact tolerances the new thread

normally is stronger than the original one.

Use in machine-building, electrical, automotive,

medical and aerospace industries.

## Description

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 6 x 1.0

With this BaerCoil® thread repair-set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in M 6 x 1.0.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair kit contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool, tang breaker and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, according to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 6 |
| Pitch | 1,0 |
| Dimension | M 6 x 1,0 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 9 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 6 mm=9 mm<br>The nominal diameter for M 6 is 6 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | M: Metric ISO standard thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 6 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 9 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 7,17 mm - 7,95 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 12,50 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 13,50 mm |

### Content

- 1 x 16163: BaerCoil HSS twist drill bit 6.30 mm
- 1 x B3009-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 6 x 1.0 EG
- 1 x EBW06: BaerCoil Installation tool M 6 x 1.0
- 1 x BZ006: BaerCoil Tang breaker M 6 x 1.0
- 20 x B7209-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 6 x 1.0 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair kit contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool, tang breaker and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, according to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

## M7 X 1.0 BaerCoil Kit (Helicoil Type)

**$67.00** ~~~~

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 7 x 1.0

* * *

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind hole threads in M 7 x 1.0.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair kit contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool, tang breaker and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, according to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 7 |
| Pitch | 1,0 |
| Dimension | M 7 x 1,0 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 10,5 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 7 mm=10.5 mm<br>The nominal diameter for M 7 is 7 mm |

strenght eg. aluminium alloys and magnesium alloys.

normally is stronger than the original one.

Use in machine-building, electrical, automotive,

medical and aerospace industries.

## Description

Complete BaerCoil Thread-Repair-Kit

Content:

1 x M8.3 BaerCoil Drill Bit

1 x HSSG BaerCoil Tap > ISO1-4H

1 x BaerCoil Inserting Tool

1 x BaerCoil Tang Break Tool

\+ 20 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304), lenght: 1,5 x D

BaerCoil:

\- Thread Repair of damaged or worn-out threads

\- Recovery of rejected items

\- Thread Armour Plating. For material with low shear

strenght eg. aluminium alloys and magnesium alloys.

Due to narrow and exact tolerances the new thread

normally is stronger than the original one.

Use in machine-building, electrical, automotive,

medical and aerospace industries.

## Description

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 8 x 1.25

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind-hole threads in M 8 x 1.25.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair kit contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool, tang breaker and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, according to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 8 |
| Pitch | 1,25 |
| Dimension | M 8 x 1,25 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 12 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 8 mm=12 mm<br>The nominal diameter for M 8 is 8 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | M: Metric ISO standard thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 8 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 12 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 9,45 mm - 10,35 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 16,38 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 17,63 mm |

### Content

- 1 x 16183: BaerCoil HSS twist drill bit 8.30 mm
- 1 x B3011-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 8 x 1.25 EG
- 1 x EBW08: BaerCoil Installation tool M 8 x 1.25
- 1 x BZ008: BaerCoil Tang breaker M 8 x 1,25
- 20 x B7211-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 8 x 1.25 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

BAERCOIL


## M8 X 1.25 BaerCoil Kit (Helicoil Type)

**$65.00** ~~~~

Product information

## BaerCoil Thread Repair Kit M 8 x 1.25

With this BaerCoil® thread repair set it is possible to repair through hole threads and blind-hole threads in M 8 x 1.25.

BaerCoil® thread inserts are the best solution for all your thread repair needs! With them you are able to make durable and strong connections. With the inserts you avoid scrap in your components and can recycle them. The inserts are precise and wear resistant - your screw will stay firmly in place without the thread insert slipping out.

The BaerCoil® thread insert is the perfect solution for damaged threads without changing the nominal diameter. For the thread repair with wire thread inserts, the thread is drilled out and a new STI thread (screw thread insert) is cut for the wire thread insert. This thread is often also called STI thread (STI=Screw Thread Insert). Then the BaerCoil® thread insert is screwed into the old thread and thus the workpieces are screwed back together. With BaerCoil® thread inserts, the thread produced is significantly more stable than the original thread.

Our thread inserts ensure that both static and dynamic work loads are distributed evenly over the individual thread turns. In addition, the flexibility of the thread inserts compensates for possible pitch and angular errors, so that optimum force transmission from the bolt to the nut thread is achieved. Especially in lightweight constructions, BaerCoil® thread inserts help to save carrier material and to use smaller or shorter screw connections. They are already an important component in aviation and vehicle construction. They significantly save material and contribute to the conservation of resources.

For repair directly on the thread, this thread repair kit contains various auxiliary tools, such as the core drill bit, hand tap with oversize for insert thread, insertion tool, tang breaker and wire thread inserts made of stainless steel.

BaerCoil® thread inserts can be shortened, if necessary, according to the required length with a side cutter or similar.

### Dimensions

| Diameter | 8 |
| Pitch | 1,25 |
| Dimension | M 8 x 1,25 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 12 mm |
| Thread length calculation | 1.5 D means 1.5 times the diameter: 1.5 times 8 mm=12 mm<br>The nominal diameter for M 8 is 8 mm |

### Characteristics

| Product group | Wire thread inserts - Repair kits |
| Product type | BaerCoil thread repair kits |
| Thread standard | M: Metric ISO standard thread according to DIN 13 |
| Tolerance | ISO2/6H |
| Direction | Right |
| Type | free running |
| Tensile strength at room temperature | >1400 N/mm² |
| Material | Stainless Steel V2A (AISI 304, X5CrNi18-10, Material No.: 1.4301) |
| Temperature resistance | 315°C long-term<br>425°C short-term |

### Applications

All normal uses for thread repair and for thread reinforcement of through-hole and blind-hole threads.

### Technical drawing

![](https://media.baer.tools/media/vector/53/0d/f3/BaerCoil_Gewindeeinsatz_Zeichnung.svg)

| Diameter | 8 |
| Length | 1,5 D |
| T (Length when installed) | 12 mm |
| F (Min. - Max. outside diameter of thread insert) | 9,45 mm - 10,35 mm |
| P (depth) | The thread insert must sit 1/4 - 1/2 turns below the surface |
| B (thread depth with chamfer) | 16,38 mm |
| D (minimum depth of the core hole, without tip) | 17,63 mm |

### Content

- 1 x 16183: BaerCoil HSS twist drill bit 8.30 mm
- 1 x B3011-1: BaerCoil HSSG single-cut tap M 8 x 1.25 EG
- 1 x EBW08: BaerCoil Installation tool M 8 x 1.25
- 1 x BZ008: BaerCoil Tang breaker M 8 x 1,25
- 20 x B7211-15: BaerCoil thread inserts M 8 x 1.25 - length: 1.5 D - type: "free running" - material: A2 (1.4301) - tolerance ISO 2 (6H)

Style

- TRS M8 X 1.25 KIT
- BAERCOIL M8 X 1.25 KIT

BAERCOIL


## M9 X 1.25 BaerCoil Kit (Helicoil Type)

**$71.00** ~~~~

Complete BaerCoil Thread-Repair-Kit

Content:

1 x M9.3 BaerCoil Drill Bit

1 x HSSG BaerCoil Tap > ISO1-4H

1 x BaerCoil Inserting Tool

1 x BaerCoil Tang Break Tool

\+ 15 BaerCoil Wire-Thread-Inserts "free running", stainless steel (ASIS 304), lenght: 1,5 x D

BaerCoil:

\- Thread Repair of damaged or worn-out threads

\- Recovery of rejected items

\- Thread Armour Plating. For material with low shear

strenght eg. aluminium alloys and magnesium alloys.

Due to narrow and exact tolerances the new thread

normally is stronger than the original one.

Use in machine-building, electrical, automotive,

medical and aerospace industries.
